\begin{problem}

Compute the following integral:

\input{Integral-Compute-0054.HELP.tex}

\[
\int{{\frac{8 \, x^{2} - 69 \, x + 40}{{\left(x - 2\right)} {\left(x - 4\right)}^{2}}}\;dx} = \answer{{\frac{54}{x - 4} - \frac{33}{2} \, \log\left(x - 2\right) + \frac{49}{2} \, \log\left(x - 4\right)}+C}
\]
\end{problem}}%}

\begin{problem}

Compute the following integral:

\input{Integral-Compute-0054.HELP.tex}

\[
\int{{\frac{4 \, {\left(x^{2} + 5 \, x - 6\right)}}{{\left(x + 8\right)} {\left(x + 7\right)} {\left(x + 4\right)}}}\;dx} = \answer{{18 \, \log\left(x + 8\right) - \frac{32}{3} \, \log\left(x + 7\right) - \frac{10}{3} \, \log\left(x + 4\right)}+C}
\]
\end{problem}}%}

\]
\end{problem}}%}

\]
\end{problem}}%}
